Nowadays , public transport has become a malr topic .
The idea of leaving public transportation aside is wdiely supported in developed countries , but this idea is rejected in developing countries , like the one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car advancing have increased over the last decades reducing the impact of people using public transport .
The possibility of travelling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even wirse , the sense of wasting time in a long value .
Nevertheless , you have another sidd to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by many other means of transportation than the ones provided by the local government .
There are countries where cars is so expensive that people choose to pay the bus car rather than paying for a full tank .
Similarly , people in countries with less work turn to these services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the sxge people give it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in others where they will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People need easy , safe and cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier then taking a train or a bus .
It 's just start your house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , catryinf weights , or suffering because of the rwkn or the snow .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't like to drive , you can find rasier to take a public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can relax listening to the music and looking around , or reading newspapers and books .
Is this car daster the public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same kevl .
Sometimes cars are faster then buses , sometimes buses are faster .
Speed trains are always faster than cars .
Speaking about money ? travelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buying the car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , maybe cars are not so cheap .
In fact , in every aspect there are pros and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the cities ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if travelling by car can be more convenient at a personal place , public transport has to be preserved by good citizens and sgrojgly sipportec by governments .

Global warming and its consequences in 2015
The Gjarduan 's article " Nature 's climate about to enter ' uncharted territory ' as it passes 1C of warming " , published on the 9rh laugh 2015 , describes the problems of global warming .
Referring to scientists at the British Met Office , 2015 is going to be the year when the milestone of 1C warming will be broken - caused by global warming - which will lead to unonown consequences on the future .
The World Meteorolovicaql Organization made known publicly that 2015 has been the hottest year on record as well as it has caused more carbon dioxide on average by bufnnig fossil fyels .
These problems just announced recently will be issues to talk about at the UN summit in Paris in three weeks .

When we imagine future , we really imagine ovecrrowded uses and eusty subway trains .

A car allows us to move faster and not to depend on others .
Travelling by car is also much more convenient .

In my opinion , it is not true .
Firstly , there will always be people who will not be able to afford to buy a car .
Students , children for large families , old people will continue to use public transportation for a long time .
Secondly , cars can also turn into public transport .

nyne can use the nearest car he or she ses .
Thirdly , people do not have an inborn driving skill , so even in the future children and teenagers will need public transportation .
This is also true for older people , who lose the ability to drive as they age .
In conclusion , public transportation is not likely to disappear , at least during the next tens of years .
